# Analysis of US By County #

For the US counties analysis, the list of all 3,143 counties (or equivalent) is sorted by the absolute number of deaths from highest to lowest.  This sorted list is then divided into two parts: counties with populations of 50,000 or more and smaller counties.

## Larger Population Counties ##

There were 990 larger population counties with a combined population of 288,662,059 (87.94% of the US population).  In these counties there have been 121,821 deaths (422.021 deaths/million) and 3,906,876 confirmed cases (13534.430 confirmed cases/million).  This group accounts for 80.65% of all US deaths and for 87.04% of all US cases.

24.20% of this group's deaths (19.52% of the total US deaths) occured in 12 counties in 9 states with a combined population of 32,573,893 (9.92% of the total US population):



The next 25.70% of this group's deaths (20.73% of the total US deaths) occured in 33 counties in 14 states with a combined population of 37,489,714 (11.42% of the total US population):



The next 25.00% of this group's deaths (20.16% of the total US deaths) occured in 82 counties in 29 states with a combined population of 67,932,348 (20.70% of the total US population)

The remaining 25.10% of this group's deaths (20.25% of the total US deaths) occured in 863 counties in 50 states with a combined population of 150,666,104 (45.90% of the total US population) 

## Smaller Population Counties ##

There were 2152 smaller population counties with a combined population of 39,577,464 (12.06% of the US population).  In these counties there have been 8,902 deaths (224.926 deaths/million) and 388,811 confirmed cases (9824.050 confirmed cases/million).  This group accounts for 5.89% of all US deaths and for 8.66% of all US cases.

24.72% of this group's deaths (1.46% of the total US deaths) occured in 53 counties in 16 states with a combined population of 1,701,512 (0.52% of the total US population):



The next 25.21% of this group's deaths (1.49% of the total US deaths) occured in 106 counties in 26 states with a combined population of 3,276,669 (1.00% of the total US population):



The next 24.99% of this group's deaths (1.47% of the total US deaths) occured in 216 counties in 32 states with a combined population of 5,279,922 (1.61% of the total US population)

The remaining 25.07% of this group's deaths (1.48% of the total US deaths) occured in 1,777 counties in 47 states with a combined population of 29,319,361 (8.93% of the total US population)
